Benchmarks for decomposition¶

RandomizedPCA-arcene¶

Benchmark setup

from sklearn.decomposition import RandomizedPCA
from deps import load_data

kwargs = {'random_state': 0, 'n_components': 9}
X, y, X_t, y_t = load_data('arcene')
obj = RandomizedPCA(**kwargs)

Benchmark statement

obj.fit(X)

   336                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   337                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   338
   339                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   340                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   341
   342                                                   Parameters
   343                                                   ----------
   344                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   345                                                       Training set.
   346
   347                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   348                                                       Target values.
   349
   350                                                   Returns
   351                                                   -------
   352                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   353                                                       Transformed array.
   354
   355                                                   """
   356                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   357                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   358                                                   if y is None:
   359                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   360                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   361                                                   else:
   362                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   363                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

RandomizedPCA-madelon¶

Benchmark setup

from sklearn.decomposition import RandomizedPCA
from deps import load_data

kwargs = {'random_state': 0, 'n_components': 9}
X, y, X_t, y_t = load_data('madelon')
obj = RandomizedPCA(**kwargs)

Benchmark statement

obj.fit(X)

   336                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   337                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   338
   339                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   340                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   341
   342                                                   Parameters
   343                                                   ----------
   344                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   345                                                       Training set.
   346
   347                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   348                                                       Target values.
   349
   350                                                   Returns
   351                                                   -------
   352                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   353                                                       Transformed array.
   354
   355                                                   """
   356                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   357                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   358                                                   if y is None:
   359                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   360                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   361                                                   else:
   362                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   363                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

Line #      Hits         Time  Per Hit   % Time  Line Contents

   200                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **params):
   201                                                   """Fit the model with X and apply the dimensionality reduction on X.
   202
   203                                                   Parameters
   204                                                   ----------
   205                                                   X : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_features)
   206                                                       Training data, where n_samples in the number of samples
   207                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   208
   209                                                   Returns
   210                                                   -------
   211                                                   X_new : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   212
   213                                                   """
   214                                                   U, S, V = self._fit(X, **params)
   215                                                   U = U[:, :self.n_components]
   216
   217                                                   if self.whiten:
   218                                                       # X_new = X * V / S * sqrt(n_samples) = U * sqrt(n_samples)
   219                                                       U *= np.sqrt(X.shape[0])
   220                                                   else:
   221                                                       # X_new = X * V = U * S * V^T * V = U * S
   222                                                       U *= S[:self.n_components]
   223
   224                                                   return U

   214                                                   U, S, V = self._fit(X, **params)
   215                                                   U = U[:, :self.n_components]
   216
   217                                                   if self.whiten:
   218                                                       # X_new = X * V / S * sqrt(n_samples) = U * sqrt(n_samples)
   219                                                       U *= np.sqrt(X.shape[0])
   220                                                   else:
   221                                                       # X_new = X * V = U * S * V^T * V = U * S
   222                                                       U *= S[:self.n_components]
   223
   224                                                   return U

   193                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **params):
   194                                                   """Fit the model from data in X and transform X.
   195
   196                                                   Parameters
   197                                                   ----------
   198                                                   X: array-like, shape (n_samples, n_features)
   199                                                       Training vector, where n_samples in the number of samples
   200                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   201
   202                                                   Returns
   203                                                   -------
   204                                                   X_new: array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   205                                                   """
   206                                                   self.fit(X, **params)
   207
   208                                                   X_transformed = self.alphas_ * np.sqrt(self.lambdas_)
   209
   210                                                   if self.fit_inverse_transform:
   211                                                       self._fit_inverse_transform(X_transformed, X)

   213                                                   return X_transformed

Line #      Hits         Time  Per Hit   % Time  Line Contents
==============================================================
   462                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None):
   463                                                   """Learn a NMF model for the data X and returns the transformed data.
   464
   465                                                   This is more efficient than calling fit followed by transform.
   466
   467                                                   Parameters
   468                                                   ----------
   469
   470                                                   X: {array-like, sparse matrix}, shape = [n_samples, n_features]
   471                                                       Data matrix to be decomposed
   472
   473                                                   Returns
   474                                                   -------
   475                                                   data: array, [n_samples, n_components]
   476                                                       Transformed data
   477                                                   """
   478         1          226    226.0      0.0          X = atleast2d_or_csr(X)
   479         1          127    127.0      0.0          check_non_negative(X, "NMF.fit")
   480
   481         1            4      4.0      0.0          n_samples, n_features = X.shape
   482
   483         1            3      3.0      0.0          if not self.n_components:
   484                                                       self.n_components = n_features
   485
   486         1         4118   4118.0      0.2          W, H = self._init(X)
   487
   488         1          130    130.0      0.0          gradW = (np.dot(W, np.dot(H, H.T))
   489         1          251    251.0      0.0                   - safe_sparse_dot(X, H.T, dense_output=True))
   490         1          134    134.0      0.0          gradH = (np.dot(np.dot(W.T, W), H)
   491         1          280    280.0      0.0                   - safe_sparse_dot(W.T, X, dense_output=True))
   492         1          272    272.0      0.0          init_grad = norm(np.r_[gradW, gradH.T])
   493         1           13     13.0      0.0          tolW = max(0.001, self.tol) * init_grad  # why max?
   494         1            3      3.0      0.0          tolH = tolW
   495
   496       201          670      3.3      0.0          for n_iter in xrange(1, self.max_iter + 1):
   497                                                       # stopping condition
   498                                                       # as discussed in paper
   499       200        39557    197.8      1.6              proj_norm = norm(np.r_[gradW[np.logical_or(gradW < 0, W > 0)],
   500       200        62081    310.4      2.5                                     gradH[np.logical_or(gradH < 0, H > 0)]])
   501       200         2396     12.0      0.1              if proj_norm < self.tol * init_grad:
   502                                                           break

   548                                                   """Transform the data X according to the fitted NMF model
   549
   550                                                   Parameters
   551                                                   ----------
   552
   553                                                   X: {array-like, sparse matrix}, shape = [n_samples, n_features]
   554                                                       Data matrix to be transformed by the model
   555
   556                                                   Returns
   557                                                   -------
   558                                                   data: array, [n_samples, n_components]
   559                                                       Transformed data
   560                                                   """
   561                                                   X = atleast2d_or_csr(X)

   563                                                   for j in xrange(0, X.shape[0]):
   564                                                       H[j, :], _ = nnls(self.components_.T, X[j, :])

   490         2          268    134.0      0.0          gradH = (np.dot(np.dot(W.T, W), H)

   492         2          542    271.0      0.0          init_grad = norm(np.r_[gradW, gradH.T])

   500       400       146068    365.2      2.9                                     gradH[np.logical_or(gradH < 0, H > 0)]])

   502                                                           break

   336                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   337                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   338
   339                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   340                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   341
   342                                                   Parameters
   343                                                   ----------
   344                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   345                                                       Training set.

   348                                                       Target values.

   350                                                   Returns
   351                                                   -------
   352                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   353                                                       Transformed array.
   354
   355                                                   """
   356                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   357                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   358                                                   if y is None:
   359                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   360                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   361                                                   else:

   363                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

   691                                               def transform(self, X, y=None):
   692                                                   """Encode the data as a sparse combination of the dictionary atoms.
   693
   694                                                   Coding method is determined by the object parameter
   695                                                   `transform_algorithm`.
   696
   697                                                   Parameters
   698                                                   ----------
   699                                                   X : array of shape (n_samples, n_features)
   700                                                       Test data to be transformed, must have the same number of
   701                                                       features as the data used to train the model.
   702
   703                                                   Returns
   704                                                   -------
   705                                                   X_new : array, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   706                                                       Transformed data
   707
   708                                                   """
   709                                                   # XXX : kwargs is not documented
   710                                                   X = array2d(X)
   711                                                   n_samples, n_features = X.shape
   712
   713                                                   code = sparse_encode(
   714                                                       X, self.components_, algorithm=self.transform_algorithm,
   715                                                       n_nonzero_coefs=self.transform_n_nonzero_coefs,
   716                                                       alpha=self.transform_alpha, n_jobs=self.n_jobs)
   717
   718                                                   if self.split_sign:
   719                                                       # feature vector is split into a positive and negative side
   720                                                       n_samples, n_features = code.shape
   721                                                       split_code = np.empty((n_samples, 2 * n_features))
   722                                                       split_code[:, :n_features] = np.maximum(code, 0)
   723                                                       split_code[:, n_features:] = -np.minimum(code, 0)
   724                                                       code = split_code
   725
   726                                                   return code

   336                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   337                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it
   338
   339                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   340                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   341
   342                                                   Parameters
   343                                                   ----------
   344                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   345                                                       Training set.
   346
   347                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   348                                                       Target values.
   349
   350                                                   Returns
   351                                                   -------
   352                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   353                                                       Transformed array.
   354
   355                                                   """
   356                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   357                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   358                                                   if y is None:
   359                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   360                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   361                                                   else:
   362                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   363                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)
